<Author>SHBD
<Content>Great Hotel, Great Location! We stayed at Hotel MonteCarlo from Oct 10 - 13, 2005 for our Honeymoon after reading reviews on TripAdvisor. We took the Aerobus for 3.60 Euros per person to Playa de Catalunya. It was a 5 minute walk to the hotel on La Rambla. The hotel is in a great location and very easy to find after a long day of exploring. We had room 412 facing La Rambla. It was great to open the balcony door and listen to the activity going on below us. Very quiet with the glass door closed. The room was very nice and clean. Bathroom was a good size with jacuzzi tub. We had a little sitting room area. The beds were sooo comfortable. Having the adjustable feature was nice for reading in bed. As many already mentioned it can get a bit uncomfortable if you end up in the crack as the beds are two double beds pushed together. We received a bottle of Champagne for our honeymoon which we enjoyed very much. We did not have breakfast at the Hotel. Instead, there is a supermarket across from the Hotel where we bought fruit and yogurt for breakfast and enjoyed it on the Solarium on the 6th floor. Our only complaint would be that we were charged an additional night as we got bumped on our connecting flight and did not make it in to Barcelona until the following day. I was able to email the Hotel from the airport as soon as we knew we could not make the flight but because we had missed their 24 hour cancellation window by about 6 hours, they charged us anyway and would not budge. We would however, definitely stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Just Fantastic!! What a fantastic hotel! I stayed here last weekend with my 80-year old mother and the staff couldn't have been nicer. They spoke excellent English and recommended and booked restaurants for us (all of which we would go to again). The hotel was spotlessly clean and the bathrooms were fabulous. I will stay at Hotel Montecarlo, again, and again, when returning to Barcelona. <Author>Dmun
<Content>Refinement, quality and great value We stayed for 4 nights and everything was perfect. Clean, modern, well presented and spacious rooms. It is a hotel with some history that has been tastefully modernised. Perfect. The hotel has real touch of class and is not too big - which means that the staff know who you are and make sure your needs are met fully without being intrusive. The language skills of the staff are excellent - speaking a range of languages. Nothing was ever too much bother for the staff - I cannot praise them enough. Check-in and check-out was very smooth. The sun terrace on the roof was a nice touch and offered a chance to relax outdoors. The public areas/ lifts/ bar etc are immaculate. Free internet access in the lobby is a bonus but you may need to wait as there is only 1 PC. The location is excellent on La Rambla. Right between 2 metro stops and close to Catalunya Square. Some travel reviews of Barcelona paint a grim/ dangerous picture of the marina/ beach area and the bottom end of La Rambla. I guess these journalists have never stepped far outside Kensington on their travels. These areas are also fantastic. Never saw any problems with crime etc and can testify that there has been a high level of investment in these areas and that they are lovely. Sound proofing in the room was excellent as we never heard any noises from the main street. We had a room with a jacuzi, robes, marble floor in the bathroom etc. Although I did not see the next room down in price I would probably not pay the extra 拢35 per night next time as I'm sure the other rooms are also great.I would definitely go back to Barcelona and would definitely recomend the Montecarlo.Loads of great places to eat in Barcelona but it does pay to get away from La Rambla if possible as the quality seems to improve for the same prices. Went to see FC Barcelona play in the Champions league - it was easy to get tickets even on the day of the game by buying them at the stadium (pices from 28 euros per seat - we bought excellent seat fro 46 euros each).

<Author>Members
<Content>Good value ! Stayed 4 nights at the beginning of October after reading the previous reviews. Well presented building from the front which looks good at night. Stayed in Pedralbes Room (room 104) which exceeded our expectations for a 3* hotel. Very clean  spacious, good bathroom, a little tight on wardrobe space but okay for short stays. The room has a nice little private decked terrace at the rear of the hotel so is away from Ramblas and quiet, good for some fresh air ! Very good staff. The room could do with its own tea / coffee making facilities. The hotel is about two thirds of the way up Ramblas (right opposite Le Meridien) so not as much hustle and bustle as the bottom end near the marina. The hotel has no restaurant but when in Barcelona your probably going to be out and about anyway and there is plenty to choose from.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A wonderful hotel!!!! My husband and I stayed at the Montecarlo for four nights in mid September and found it to be very well located, nicely appointed, clean, spacious, and to have very friendly and helpful employees. Upon noticing on our arrival that our luggage had not arrived on our flight, they took the initiative to take a copy of our reference documents and look into it for us. We received the luggage the next day. The staff was in a word, excellent, and they all spoke great English. They recommended great restaurants too! I agree with others' comments that the hotel should have a higher rating than 3 stars. We felt it was an excellent value for the price.The staff made a nice gesture to me as I celebrated my birthday while staying there, which they discovered from my passport, it was a lovely touch.This has absolutely nothing to do with the hotel, but please watch your purses/wallets extremely closely while in Barcelona, I had my purse stolen while sitting at Farga cafe (just down the street and around the corner) having a cappucino about 11:00 one evening, and in retrospect am fairly sure that the waiter there was in on it. Also, if you have time and transportation, I highly recommend a side trip to Roses and/or Cadeques, two charming coastal towns north of Barcelona. Sign me thrilled in Virginia

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Favorite Hotel in Eurpoe My fiance and I stayed at Hotel Montecarlo for four nights. We stayed in seven hotels in Europe and Hotel Montecarlo was our favorite. The staff is extremely helpful and friendly. They greeted us with maps and brochures about events in the city. The location is wonderful, walking distance to most site and the metro. I love the crisp, clean, white, soft bed linens and the modern well designed bathroom. Breakfast was wonderful but a little pricy at 14 eruos each. I can not wait to return to Barcelona and stay at Hotel Montecarlo!

<Author>Anonymous046
<Content>The lap of luxury We stayed here for one night as the 5* hotel we had booked with were unable to house us for the night due to refurbishment. We were told that this was a lower class hotel so they booked us in to a suite. I am now astonished to read that Montecarlo is only a 3* hotel, as it was head and shoulders above the 5* hotel we had booked. The service was impeccable. The doorman came up to show us how all the mod cons worked, and we were handed a map and various leaflets about events and attractions in the city upon arrival. We were also recommended several restaurants (she wrote all the names on the map for us), and the Tapas restaurant that she said was her favourite turned out to be a treat. The room was utterly fantastic. It was cool and spacious, with no street noise whatsoever, despite the location on the bustling La Rambla. The room was stylish and sophisticated, with plenty of storage, and overlooked a pretty courtyard. We had electrically adjustable beds and electric blinds that were operated from the bedside. The small living room area was comfortable, and the mini bar was extremely good value (around 1.5 euros for a soft drink - as opposed to 5 euros in the 5* hotel we were in for the rest of our stay!). The best feature was the fantastic jacuzzi, a wonderful touch and very relaxing. The hydrotherapy shower was a little baffling but I wish we had stayed there a little longer so that I could have worked it out! I felt like we had our own little paradise amongst the heat and mania of the city, and if I were to return to Barcelona, I would without a doubt stay here.Great location, wonderful staff, fabulous rooms.... Book now!

If we ever return to Barcelona, I will not even bother to research hotels...this is my choice hands down!

The bath featured attractive salmon-colored marble tile, a wood veneer ceiling, full size tub with shower and whirlpool, and bidet. Matching bathrobes and slippers added an accent of luxury.There鈥檚 also a rooftop 鈥渟olarium鈥?with chaise lounges and a view of Las Ramblas below. <Content>Lovely hotel, perfect location I stayed in this hotel at the start of my honeymoon this May based on what I had read in Tripadvisor. Having looked at the website I e-mailed the hotel to find out about making a booking and mentioned we were starting our honeymoon... I received an e-mail giving me a discount on their top room -Making it cheaper than the one I was going to book! When we checked in, we received champagne and strawberries and a congratulatory note from the staff. The hotel itself is at the top of Las Ramblas which is a perfect location - there are lots of shops, restaurants and bars nearby. The open top tour bus routes both run from the top of the road and there are about three metro stations on this street.Our room was a suite which had a jacuzzi bath and a steam and sauna shower - It was great when we worked out how to use it! The beds are remote control comfort beds and were amazingly comfortable! The staff were friendly and very honest - I actually received a call having left the hotel about a top I had left behind beside the bin in a plastic bag to throw away...I would definitely recommend this hotel to any one...

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Super hotel booked the hotel after reading up on it in tripadvisor.com. I booked direct with hotel who answered e mails quickly. I asked for a quiet room and was given one. It was at back of hotel and the view was of a wall - however we got the peace and quiet we asked for. There was a quiet rumble from the Metro trains every few minutes but with aircon on it was not that noticeable although did take a little getting used to.We had a Gracia room on Floor 1. Gracia rooms have a small sitting room attached with armchairs, CD player and TV. Beds were comfortable and the bathroom was luxury with a superb shower and separate jacuzzi bath.The front desk staff were friendly, polite and more than helpful. They spent ages helping my son find a skateboard shop in Barcelona!We were careful and had no problems with pickpockets. They are around but then so are the police who were constantly patrolling Las Ramblas/Catalunya. We walked miles and travelled daily on Metro and had no problems. Just keep on guard.For a 3 star in a super location this hotel is to be recommended.

<Content>Hotel Montecarlo is Fabulous We stayed at the Montecarlo May 22, 2005. I chose this hotel after reading other reviews on Trip Advisor. I must say they were right on! This was a very good find, and I highly recommend this hotel.

<Author>duxfans
<Content>What a value This hotel was so much more than expected. Even upon first entering the marble front steps and marble pillars, you have to be impressed. I have stayed in many 3 star properties and this one has to be the finest. There are 2 elevators, an empressive lobby, a bar, and a breakfast room on the main floor. There is a beautiful sitting room on the next floor, with a view of Las Ramblas. The rooms are well appointed with 10 foot ceilings with beautiful crown moldings. The adjustable bed is extremely comfortable. There are double windows, each with double pain glass to keep out all of the noise and an electric shade in between them that will completely darken the room. With a mini bar, a jacuzzi tub, t.v. with ppv movies, robes, it has all of the amenities of a higher rated hotel. The staff was extemely helpful and friendly. The location couldn't have been better, just 5 minutes up Las Ramblas to Placa Catalunya. I can't wait to go back and stay there again. And they can keep my pajamas.

<Author>jameshome
<Content>Hard to imagine a better home base in Barcelona the Montecarlo was just out of our price range, but we came close to saving the difference bynever needing to take public transportation; the location is in the very heart of Barcelona, and almost everything we wanted to see was a beautiful walk away. we had a Sants room, which was large, modern and luxurious. the staff was friendly and competent, took care of making sure our cab was there and waiting for us at 3am when it was time to go to the train station, and just generally made it an incredibly comfortable stay.nitty gritty: standard but relatively reasonably priced mini bar, standard safe, good size closet in separate dressing area, double paned windows, bidet and jacuzzi.complaints? no balcony (although many other Montecarlo rooms have them and I should have just asked for one), which made the Montecarlo's incredible view of The Ramblas and Barcelona a little torturous each night that the sun did that really amazing thing. there's a roof deck, but it closes before sunset, which I suppose keeps it from becoming a party up there, but man were we bummed when we headed up there with a jug of sangria. just one more: the adjustable beds were pretty entertaining, and great for waking up and lying around reading guidebooks, but there's no getting around the fact that two single beds pushed up next to each other are kind of irritating if you are the kind of couple who sleeps curled up with each other. I fell off in the middle more than once!I will strongly recommend the Montecarlo to my friends and family who visit Barcelona, and look forward to returning there sometime soon!

<Author>Elke1171
<Content>Could not have asked for more My husband and I stayed here in February 2005 for a weekend city break after reading other TripAidvsor reviews. The location is ideal - only a two/three minute walk from the main bus and underground stations at Placa de Catalunya and centrally located on La Ramblas. The staff were very friendly and inviting on arrival and could not have done more to help. They even remembered our room number when we returned from our day out on the second day to hand us our room key. Our room was very comfortable and clean, not especially spacious, but they seem to have thought of everything as far as amenities are concerned (adjustomatic beds, jacuzzi bath, bidet, mini-bar etc.). We did not have a view from our room window, but we spent most of our time exploring Barcelona anyway. Breakfast was very nice with a good self-service selection and the staff would bring freshly-squeezed orange juice to your table and your choice of tea (they had a huge selection of teas) or coffee. Overall it was an excellent base to explore this beautiful city and we could not have asked for more for the price we paid. Would definitely recommend it.

<Author>snooky
<Content>Good Hotel... Great position/view We went to this hotel during December with my daughter aged 9 for her birthday. We booked a junior suite, which consisted of a bedroom, a separate living area, a little patio and a shower/hydro sauna combination with a jacuzzi in the bathroom. The most annoying factor was that when I'd booked this online, I had made a request for an extra bed for a child in the comments section, I even phoned up SRS to make sure that this was possible for the room type we'd booked as you couldn't specify a child occuping a room with parents on line. When we arrived at the hotel however, they claimed that they had not been informed and had no record of such a request. What appeared to be manager of the day made a bit of huff and puff about putting in an extra bed (rollaway style). This was a little annoying, particularly as it was my little daughters birthday present. I also thought it bad form that they charge full adult rate for an extra (rollaway) bed being put in (about $50 per night if my memory serves me correctly), particularly in a suite where you have a separate 'living area' anyway. Though reading through the fine print once you've booked, they do say children over 3 are charged at the full rate.Eventually it was sorted it out however, and the room was nice enough, though I thought a little dark, as it was on the side of the hotel.. it did have a little balcony which was nice. The decor was a little brown/white and minimilist for my liking. I would have liked tea/coffee making facilities in the room as well, but we did order snack/drinks via room service and it was fine.The general staff were pleasant and helpful. The hydrosauna is fun, however, the instructions are not great.. it took us a little time to work out how to get a steam room effect in it.. and you have to wait quite a while for it to get going (we though it wasn't working)...The hydromassage takes some working out as well.. we all got hydromassaged heads.. because we couldn't work out how to stop the 'top' jets (suitable for very tall people I think!).They do need to put some new plastic instructions into the shower as the ones inside are worn away in parts. The view from the hotel is just fanstastic.... Barcelona bustling and all the mime artists in the middle boulevard, and you are SO in the middle of it all. A short walk to the cathedral, which at Xmas was nice with the market. The metro stop is close at hand as well, handy for visiting all the spots.Overall, a good hotel, reasonable rooms, great position.  
<Date>Feb 15, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>There is absolutely nothing negative to say about this hotel You don't even have to think about it. Just book this hotel. This was my 6th trip to Barcelona, and I travel extensively throughout Europe. I have never had a more positive hotel experience for this price range. I booked the hotel for 115 euros (an Internet special) and was ready to ask and pay for an upgrade after I arrived and could see the room. I didn't need to - the room was perfect. Spacious (for Europe), quiet despite having two large windows (double paned, completely noise-proof), sparsely but chic'ly decorated (like a boutique hotel). The beds were soft and so comfortable, with good linens. The bathroom was large and clean, with Jacuzzi tub.The best thing about this hotel is the location. It's across the street from the covered food market, and we had a delightful experience getting up and stumbling literally across the way to have a breakfast made on-the-spot from fresh local produce, meats, and eggs. You are within a short walk from everything you could possibly need or want - the harbor, the Placa Catalunya, two metro stops, the Old Town, and a multitude of restaurants and shops and bars/discos.I will never stay anywhere else in Barcelona. I would change my dates of travel just to be able to get a place in this hotel!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Montecarlo saved our Honeymoon My husband and I spent one night at Hotel Montecarlo as an extra weekend trip to our honeymoon cruise. We chose this hotel because of it's location and we wanted to maximize our sightseeing time. We checked in at 8:30 in the morning and they were ready with a smile. The room was on the top floor, very cozy and tastefully decorated. The marble bathroom and jetted tub were wonderful! The bed was so comfortable, and we were so exhausted, so we took a quick nap. We then headed out for some sightseeing around 11am. The hotel's location right on Las Ramblas is perfect. Everything is within a manageable walking distance. Unfortunately, within our first 10 minutes on a very crowded metro, my husband was pickpocketed. (Beware! I've never seen such absolute professionals!) We tried to find the culprit, but of course it was impossible. We returned to the hotel immediately. The staff was great and offered to call our different credit card companies for us. The gave us a map and great directions to the police station. All in all, they were very helpful and very apologetic that this had happened to us in their city. We spent our entire first day trying to do damage control with credit cards and bank accounts, and then tried to do a little sight seeing. We returned later that evening. The front desk staff had changed shifts by then, but they were still as helpful and friendly as ever. As soon as we walked in, even the young lady at the front desk immediately asked us if everything was alright and if we needed any additional help. We thanked her then went on to our room to relax a bit before dinner. Within 5 minutes of being in our room, there was a knock at the door. The front desk had had a beautiful fruit basket and a nice bottle of chilled champagne brought up to us. Again, they apologized that we had been robbed in their city and hoped that this 'small gesture' would help in some way. After feeling so violated and distraught all day, and glancing warily at every passerby, it was so nice to know that someone wanted to be kind to us! The next day, the hotel even held our bags for hours after we checked out, just so we would have a safe place to keep our things and still get to see the city. What was to be a dream trip to Barcelona turned into a temporary nightmare. Thanks to a few thoughtful people at Hotel Montecarlo, it still turned out to be a wonderful end to our honeymoon. I DEFINITELY recommend Hotel Montecarlo to anyone wanting to thoroughly enjoy their trip in Barcelona. It made the difference for us.  
<Date>Dec 12, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A standard 3-star property nothing more We stayed in the Montecarlo for two nights (December 3-5). We got a good deal through the SRS website which included a free room upgrade (if available). First of all, the information the hotel give on their website is a complete lie. They claim all rooms have adjustable beds and massage tubs. That is NOT TRUE! They have something called the standard room which has none of these facilities. Secondly, the free room upgrade did not exist according to the staff (I had it on print but they said no!) but if I paid an extra 30 euro a night then they would upgrade me. They said bad information about the information on their website and that was it. After getting very pissed off I got the deal worked out that we stay one night in the standard room and one night in an upgraded room without extra charge. The standard rooms is nothing but a small room with a rather uncomfortable bed. In my opinion, the standard room is representable for a 2-star hotel and nothing more. The upgrade room was a lot better, bigger and brighter with adjustable beds and a water jet tub. The beds were very comfortable and is it one thing I care about in hotels then it is the bed. The room was also very quiet. The staff is a very mixed bag, one of them was very rude and arrogant while one of them was among the most serviceminded people I ever met in a hotel. If you are lucky and you get everything you have reserved without any hazzle, well, then the Montecarlo is as good as any 3-star hotel. But given all the problems I cannot recommend this hotel and the only thing that stopped me from giving it a Terrible rating is the A-class location of the hotel, that some of the staff tried really hard to fulfill their obligations and that the upgraded room was very comfortable and quiet. Go for a 4-star hotel instead, you might have to pay just a bit more but the fact is that the Montecarlo is a basic 3-star property and nothing more.  
<Date>Dec 6, 2004

<Author>Porsche_Guy
<Content>Excellent In Every Way The Hotel Montecarlo is the perfect place to stay in Barcelona. Do not let the fact that the hotel is on La Rambla dissuade you. Rather, enjoy the fact that you will have an oasis of calm in the middle of the chaos that is La Rambla. Last week we spent 3 nights at the Hotel Montecarlo. The entire experience was great; even before entiring the hotel since we were met at the curb by a polite and helpful bellman. The hotel is small by comparison to some of its local competitors with only 55 rooms, but in our view this lends an air of intimacy to the place. It does not take long to get to know the staff, and while the hotel lacks a concierge this is not a negative factor since the entire front desk staff is knowledgeable and more than willing to assist with cabs, reservations, directions and so forth. Gus, from Seattle, was particuarily delightful and helpful. Everyone on staff spoke English, and this added to the oasis quality of the hotel. Our room, no. 102, was quite large with a king sized bed in a separate bedroom, a sitting room with a bar, TV coffee table and seating for two in a bright windowed room, and a huge bathroom that included a whirlpool bathtub and a separate shower stall. The room was very well soundproofed and the AC was efficient and quiet. The Hotel Montecarlo will be our hotel of choice in Barcelona.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Amazing! Booked this hotel after reading the reviews on this site. Amazing location, right on Las Ramblas (there are 5 ramblas, this is on the Rambla Cappuccino, about a three-five minute walk from Plaza de Catalunya, where you can catch the metro). Free Internet access as you walk in, great prices for room service and great service in the bar. We met friends there nightly for a drink before going out. Staff couldn't be more helpful. We bought flowers for a friend and dropped them off at the front desk so we didn't have to carry them and they put them in water and held on to them until we came back for drinks that evening. Bathrooms are large and clean--ours had a jacuzzi tub (ask for room 201). View of the Ramlas is great--double glass doors to keep out noise. We had no problems. Radio, CD player, television, AC, minibar, comfortable beds. A+! Oh, breakfast is not included and is around $16 euro. We found great deals at cafes near by for a croissant and coffee for about 3 euro. Be sure to try some of the places off the beaten path. There are great cafes and restaurants to be found just meandering through the streets behind the Ramblas.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Definately worth a visit! I booked the Hotel Montecarlo off the back of the reviews I had read on trip advisor. I would normally head straight for a four or five star hotel for a short break to ensure we had no issues surrounding the quality of our accomodation. However, the reviews were so positive and the location seemed ideal so we decided to give it a go.The location is ideal if you want to have a base from which to explore Barcelona on foot. We found the staff to be very friendly and helpful (although they wouldn't book a taxi for us, advising us that it would be easier to flag one down outside - which it wasn't!)Breakfast was excellent, especially the scrambled eggs (just delicious) and there is a great roof patio area where you can lie and soak up some afternoon sun if your husband likes to crash out for a siesta (as mine has a tendancy to do)!The rooms were clean and smart but a little bit generic for the character of the building. This hotel isn't cheap for a three star property and from looking at the outside of the building I was hoping for a little more character in the rooms.I was also a little disapointed to find that our room was equipped with two beds pushed together rather than a kings size bed - this is no fun if you are there to celebrate your wedding anniversary!!This hotel is definately worth a visit as long as you bear these things in mind before booking.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Couldn't be Better!! The best location in Barcelona. Right on the Ramplas, but with double glazing to keep out the noise at night. Very smart rooms with electric beds  powerful jaccuzi baths. Big balcony.Excellent buffet breakfast (12 sorts of tea!)Friendly, bi-lingual staff who sort out restaurants, taxis etc.Very good prices. It's a 3 star because they havn't got a restaurant (there are many, many great restaurants in the area, anyway) and they have no disabled access (although this is being built as we write)I'd go back tomorrow!
